# <a name="office-client-application-and-platform-availability-for-office-add-ins"></a><span data-ttu-id="e1d8a-103">Application cliente Office et disponibilité de la plate-forme pour les compléments Office</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e1d8a-103">Office client application and platform availability for Office Add-ins</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e1d8a-p101">Pour fonctionner comme prévu, votre complément Office peut dépendre d'une application Office spécifique, d'un ensemble de conditions requises, d'un membre de l’API ou d'une version de l'API. Les tableaux suivants contiennent les plates-formes disponibles, les points d'extension, les ensembles de conditions requises de l’API et les API courantes qui sont actuellement prises en charge pour chaque application Office.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e1d8a-p101">To work as expected, your Office Add-in might depend on a specific Office application, a requirement set, an API member, or a version of the API. The following tables contain the available platforms, extension points, API requirement sets, and Common APIs that are currently supported for each Office application.</span></span>

<br>

|<a href="#excel"><img src="../images/index/logo-excel.svg" alt="Excel" width="48" /><br><span data-ttu-id="e1d8a-106"><span>Excel</span></a></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e1d8a-106"><span>Excel</span></a></span></span>|<a href="#onenote"><img src="../images/index/logo-onenote.svg" alt="OneNote" width="48" /><br><span data-ttu-id="e1d8a-107"><span>OneNote</span></a></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e1d8a-107"><span>OneNote</span></a></span></span>|<a href="#outlook"><img src="../images/index/logo-outlook.svg" alt="Outlook" width="48" /><br><span data-ttu-id="e1d8a-108"><span>Outlook</span></a></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e1d8a-108"><span>Outlook</span></a></span></span>|<a href="#powerpoint"><img src="../images/index/logo-powerpoint.svg" alt="PowerPoint" width="48" /><br><span data-ttu-id="e1d8a-109"><span>PowerPoint</span></a></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e1d8a-109"><span>PowerPoint</span></a></span></span>|<a href="#project"><img src="../images/index/logo-project-server.svg" alt="Project" width="48" /><br><span data-ttu-id="e1d8a-110"><span>Project</span></a></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e1d8a-110"><span>Project</span></a></span></span>|<a href="#word"><img src="../images/index/logo-word.svg" alt="Word" width="48" /><br><span data-ttu-id="e1d8a-111"><span>Word</span></a></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e1d8a-111"><span>Word</span></a></span></span>|
|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="e1d8a-112">La version initiale d’Office 2016 installée via MSI contient uniquement les ensembles de conditions ExcelApi 1.1, WordApi 1.1 et API commune.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e1d8a-112">The initial Office 2016 release installed via MSI only contains the ExcelApi 1.1, WordApi 1.1, and Common API requirement sets.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e1d8a-113">Pour plus d’informations sur l’historique de mise à jour des différentes versions d’Office, consultez la section [Voir aussi](#see-also).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e1d8a-113">For more information about the update history of the various Office versions, check out the [See also](#see-also) section.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="e1d8a-576"><sup>1</sup> Pour nécessiter le jeu d'API d'identité 1.3 dans votre code additionnel, vérifiez s'il est pris en charge en appelant `isSetSupported('IdentityAPI', '1.3')`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e1d8a-576"><sup>1</sup> To require Identity API set 1.3 in your add-in code, check if it's supported by calling `isSetSupported('IdentityAPI', '1.3')`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e1d8a-577">Le déclarer dans le manifeste de votre macro complémentaire n'est pas pris en charge.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e1d8a-577">Declaring it in your add-in's manifest isn't supported.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e1d8a-578">Vous pouvez également déterminer si l’API est prise en charge en vérifiant qu’elle n’est pas `undefined`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e1d8a-578">You can also determine if the API is supported by checking that it's not `undefined`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e1d8a-579">Pour plus d’informations, consultez [Utilisation des API d’un ensemble de conditions requises ultérieure](../reference/requirement-sets/outlook-api-requirement-sets.md#using-apis-from-later-requirement-sets).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e1d8a-579">For further details, see [Using APIs from later requirement sets](../reference/requirement-sets/outlook-api-requirement-sets.md#using-apis-from-later-requirement-sets).</span></span>
